TEGRIDY FARMS
FULL SOURCE CODE SECURITY AUDIT — 100 FINDINGS
Line-by-line review of 14,454 lines | 13 Solidity contracts + React frontend | March 2026
Executive summary
This audit identified 12 critical, 18 high, 30 medium, and 40 low severity findings across smart contracts, frontend code, and project architecture. The codebase shows security awareness (SECURITY FIX #N comments throughout), but several fixes are incomplete and the full source reveals issues invisible from the overview alone.
Top 6 critical chains: (1) votingPowerAt() ignores blockNumber — snapshot governance is theater. (2) TegridyPair charges 1% fee but UI shows 0.3% — real cost 1.3% + 5% default slippage = 6.3% per swap. (3) NFT position transfers orphan the first position permanently. (4) PremiumAccess.withdrawToTreasury drains the refund pool. (5) emergencyWithdrawPosition bypasses all lock restrictions with no access gate. (6) Zero tests across 14,454 lines of mainnet code.

              <w:t xml:space="preserve">#1 
votingPowerAt() ignores blockNumber — snapshot governance is fake
TegridyStaking.sol:13957
Issue: 
votingPowerAt(user, blockNumber) discards the blockNumber parameter and calls votingPowerOf(user) which returns current power. CommunityGrants.voteOnProposal() calls this at snapshotBlock, believing it gets historical power. Attacker buys TOWELI after proposal creation and votes with full weight.
Fix: 
Implement ERC20Votes checkpointing. Each stake/withdraw writes a checkpoint. votingPowerAt must binary-search checkpoint history.

              <w:t xml:space="preserve">#2 
NFT transfer overwrites userTokenId — positions become orphaned
TegridyStaking.sol:14160-14172
Issue: 
_update() sets userTokenId[to]=tokenId unconditionally. If Alice owns tokenId=5 and buys tokenId=8 on OpenSea, her userTokenId becomes 8 and position 5 is invisible to pendingRewardOf(), votingPowerOf(), and all frontend hooks. Funds locked until expiry with no UI path to recover.
Fix: 
Revert in _update() if userTokenId[to]!=0, or convert to array, or remove 1-position-per-address constraint.

              <w:t xml:space="preserve">#3 
PremiumAccess.withdrawToTreasury() drains the refund escrow
PremiumAccess.sol:12157-12163
Issue: 
Transfers entire token balance to treasury including tokens held for cancelSubscription() refunds. Comment admits 'simplified approach.' Owner call → subscribers can't get pro-rata refunds. Directly defeats SECURITY FIX #17.
Fix: 
Track totalRefundableBalance. Only allow withdrawal of balance minus totalRefundableBalance.

SwapFeeRouter.swapExactETHForTokens — slippage checked on wrong amount

SwapFeeRouter uses bare approve() — fails on USDT and non-standard tokens
SwapFeeRouter.sol:12696,12747
Issue: 
IERC20(path[0]).approve(address(router), amountIn) is a raw call. USDT's approve() returns void, not bool — SafeERC20 isn't used here. Will revert for USDT swaps. Also: repeated approvals without resetting to 0 first fail on tokens requiring zero-first approval.
Fix: 
Use SafeERC20.forceApprove() which handles non-standard return values and resets allowance atomically.

RevenueDistributor.claim() uses current lock for all historical epochs
RevenueDistributor.sol:12504-12516
Issue: 
Reads userLocked once at claim time, applies to ALL unclaimed epochs. User stakes 1 TOWELI at epoch 1, stakes 1M more at epoch 50, claims epochs 1-50 as if they had 1M the whole time. Massive overpayment on early epochs, theft from legitimate early stakers.

TegridyPair _mintFee sends 80% of fees to protocol, only 20% to LPs
TegridyPair.sol:13218
Issue: 
numerator uses *4 making protocol take 4/5 (80%) of fee growth. Standard Uni V2 is 1/6 (16.7%). LPs earn 5x less than on Uniswap for same liquidity. Combined with 1% total fee: 0.8% goes to protocol, 0.2% to LPs. LP flight is guaranteed.
Fix: 
Reduce to standard 1/6 protocol share. At 1% total fee: 0.17% protocol, 0.83% LPs.

RevenueDistributor.emergencyWithdraw can drain unclaimed user funds
RevenueDistributor.sol:12470-12481
Issue: 
When totalLocked==0, owner can withdraw ALL ETH including earmarked but unclaimed epoch rewards. Users who registered but haven't claimed lose their share.
Fix: 
Only withdraw balance minus totalEarmarked - totalClaimed (the excess).

PremiumAccess.cancelSubscription refund calculated on current fee rate
PremiumAccess.sol:12138
Issue: 
refundAmount = monthlyFeeToweli * remainingTime / MONTH. If owner raises monthlyFeeToweli, existing subscribers' refund increases (could exceed what they paid). If lowered, refund decreases below fair value.
Fix: 
Store the fee rate at subscription time and use that for refund calculation.

GalleryPage.tsx:9262-9284

Votes stored in localStorage per address. Clear storage → vote again. Script → thousands of votes. Different addresses → unlimited votes. If gallery rankings affect anything (bounties, commissions), this is exploitable.

              <w:t xml:space="preserve">#54 
slippageBps variable name is misleading — it's actually tenths
useSwap.ts:6902
Issue: 
slippageBps = BigInt(Math.round(slippage * 10)); divided by 1000n. This is tenths, not basis points (which would be /10000). If anyone treats it as actual bps, slippage is off by 10x.
Fix: 
Rename to slippageTenths or use actual bps: slippage * 100 / 10000.
